<div id="area_channel_layer_backdrop" class="layer_back_drop_class" style="z-index:999;position:absolute;z-index:999;left:0;top:0;display:none"></div>
<script>

    $(document).ready(function(){
        $(window).resize(function(){
            if(!$("#area_channel_layer").is(":hidden"))
            {
                setLayerPosition();
            }
        });
    });

    window.areaChannelChangeTab = function(sName, oEvent)
    {
        $("#area_channel_layer_all").children().hide();
        $("#area_channel_layer_list").children().removeClass("on");
        $(oEvent).addClass("on");
        $("#area_channel_layer_all").children("div[name='area_channel_div_" + sName + "']").show();
        $("#area_channel_layer_backdrop").show();
    };

    window.openAreaChannelLayer = function()
    {
        setLayerPosition();
        $("#area_channel_layer,#area_channel_layer_backdrop").show();
    };

    window.setLayerPosition = function()
    {
        var dl = $(document).scrollLeft();
        var dt = $(document).scrollTop();
        var ww = $(document).width();
        var dwh = $(document).height();
        var wwh = $(window).height();
        var ow = $("#area_channel_layer").width();
        var oh = $("#area_channel_layer").height();
        var fLeft = (ww - ow) / 2 + dl;
        var fTop = (wwh - oh) * 382 / 1000 + dt;//黄金比例
        $("#area_channel_layer").css({'left': Math.max(parseInt(fLeft), dl), 'top': Math.max(parseInt(fTop), dt)});
        $("#area_channel_layer_backdrop").css({'width': ww + 'px', 'height': dwh + 'px'});
    }
</script>    <div class="nag" id="topIndex">

In [34]:
text='''
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="ISO-8859-1"?>

<bookstore>

<book>
  <title lang="eng1">Harry Potter</title>
  <price>29.99</price>
</book>

<book>
  <title lang="eng2">Learning XML</title>
  <price>39.95</price>
</book>

</bookstore>
'''

from lxml import etree

root=etree.HTML(text)

root.xpath('//.')

#51job爬虫总结
import requests
from lxml import etree
from pandas import DataFrame

#确定一个对象，即网址
url='https://search.51job.com/list/010000,000000,0000,32,9,99,Java%25E5%25BC%2580%25E5%258F%2591,2,1.html'
res=requests.get(url)
res.encoding='gbk'
root=etree.HTML(res.text)

#利用xpath提取网页信息
position=root.xpath('//p[@class="t1 "]/span/a/@title')
company=root.xpath('//span[@class="t2"]/a/@title')
place=root.xpath('//div[@class="el"]/span[@class="t3"]/text()')
salary=root.xpath('//div[@class="el"]/span[@class="t4"]/text()')

#把取出的信息放到数据框
jobInfo=DataFrame([position,company,place,salary]).T
jobInfo.columns=['职位名','公司名','地点','薪资']
jobInfo.head(10)

In [73]:
#模式字符串
'''
. 匹配除了换行符之外的任意字符
* 0\1\多次
'''

string='python2016pythonpython'

pat1='py...'
r1=re.findall(pat1,string)
print(r1)

pat2='py.*'
r2=re.findall(pat2,string)
print(r2)

['pytho', 'pytho', 'pytho']
['python2016pythonpython']
In [75]:
'''
() 模式单元
? 0\1次
'''

pat3='py(.*)on' #贪婪模式——尽可能多的匹配
r3=re.findall(pat3,string)
print(r3)

['thon2016pythonpyth']
In [76]:
pat4='py(.*?)on' #非贪婪模式——尽可能少的匹配
r4=re.findall(pat4,string)
print(r4)

['th', 'th', 'th']

#51job爬虫梳理
import re
import requests
from pandas import DataFrame

url='https://search.51job.com/list/010000,000000,0000,32,9,99,Java%25E5%25BC%2580%25E5%258F%2591,2,1.html'
res=requests.get(url)
res.encoding='gbk'

#利用正则表达式提取网页信息
#职位名
pat='<a target="_blank" title="(.*)" href=".*" onmousedown=".*">'
position=re.findall(pat,res.text)
#公司名
company_pat='<span class="t2"><a target="_blank" title="(.*)" href=".*">.*</a></span>'
company=re.findall(company_pat,res.text)
#工作地点
place_pat='<div class="el">.*?<span class="t3">(.*?)</span>' #非贪婪模式
place=re.findall(place_pat,res.text,re.S)
#薪资
salary_pat='<div class="el">.*?<span class="t4">(.*?)</span>'
salary=re.findall(salary_pat,res.text,re.S)

jobinfo=DataFrame([position,company,place,salary]).T
jobinfo.columns=['职位名','公司名','地点','薪资']

'''
爬取多页信息
1、找翻页规律，构造网址
2、通过循环爬取多页信息
'''

https://search.51job.com/list/010000,000000,0000,32,9,99,Java%25E5%25BC%2580%25E5%258F%2591,2,1.html

https://search.51job.com/list/010000,000000,0000,32,9,99,Java%25E5%25BC%2580%25E5%258F%2591,2,2.html

https://search.51job.com/list/010000,000000,0000,32,9,99,Java%25E5%25BC%2580%25E5%258F%2591,2,3.html

In [109]:
#51job爬虫梳理
import re
import requests
from pandas import DataFrame
import pandas as pd

jobinfoAll=DataFrame()

for i in range(1,4):
    url='https://search.51job.com/list/010000,000000,0000,32,9,99,Java%25E5%25BC%2580%25E5%258F%2591,2,'+str(i)+'.html'
    res=requests.get(url)
    res.encoding='gbk'

    #利用正则表达式提取网页信息
    #职位名
    pat='<a target="_blank" title="(.*)" href=".*" onmousedown=".*">'
    position=re.findall(pat,res.text)
    #公司名
    company_pat='<span class="t2"><a target="_blank" title="(.*)" href=".*">.*</a></span>'
    company=re.findall(company_pat,res.text)
    #工作地点
    place_pat='<div class="el">.*?<span class="t3">(.*?)</span>' #非贪婪模式
    place=re.findall(place_pat,res.text,re.S)
    #薪资
    salary_pat='<div class="el">.*?<span class="t4">(.*?)</span>'
    salary=re.findall(salary_pat,res.text,re.S)

    jobinfo=DataFrame([position,company,place,salary]).T
    jobinfo.columns=['职位名','公司名','地点','薪资']
    jobinfoAll=pd.concat([jobinfoAll,jobinfo])

jobinfoAll.head()

In [120]:
#图片保存到本地
res=requests.get(image_url)

with open('jdpics/1.jpg','wb') as pic_object: #wb表示以二进制方式写入文件
    pic_object.write(res.content) #对于非文本请求，用res.content
In [124]:
#通过循环保存所有图片
url='https://list.jd.com/list.html?cat=9987,653,655'
res=requests.get(url)

image_pat='<img width="220" height="220" data-img="1" .*="//(.*?)">'
imagelist=re.findall(image_pat,res.text)

x=1
for imageurl in imagelist:
    imageurl='http://'+imageurl
    imagename='jdpics/'+str(x)+'.jpg'
    #图片保存到本地
    res=requests.get(imageurl)
    with open(imagename,'wb') as pic_object: #wb表示以二进制方式写入文件
        pic_object.write(res.content) #对于非文本请求，用res.content
    x+=1

其他模式字符串及正则匹配实例¶

In [125]:
#提取字符串中的数字
import re

s1="360人最近报名"
rst=re.sub("\D","",s1)
print(rst)

360
In [126]:
#匹配电话号码
s1="python0997-5252312hadoop"

pat="\d{4}-\d{7}"
r=re.findall(pat,s1)
print(r)

['0997-5252312']
In [127]:
#匹配多个电话号码
s1="python0997-5252312hadoop010-84843212spark"

pat="\d{4}-\d{7}|\d{3}-\d{8}"
r=re.findall(pat,s1)
print(r)

['0997-5252312', '010-84843212']
In [128]:
#匹配字符串中的QQ号
string="技术讨论QQ群：12345678，欢迎交流讨论"

pat="\d{5,13}"
r=re.findall(pat,string)
print(r)

['12345678']
In [129]:
#匹配网址
string="<a href='http://www.sina.com'>新浪</a>"

pat="[a-zA-Z]+://[^\s]*(?:.com|.cn)"
re.findall(pat,string)
Out[129]:
['http://www.sina.com']
In [130]:
string="<a href='http://www.python.org'>python</a>"

pat="[a-zA-Z]+://[^\s]*(?:.com|.cn|.org)"
re.findall(pat,string)
Out[130]:
['http://www.python.org']
